Talk about how there were multiple genres and multiple production companies, so we just chose the one that was most prominent.

In[]:
lst=[]
for index, row in box_office_df.iterrows():
    if type(row['production_companies'])!=str or not row['production_companies']:
        lst.append(index)
    else:
        box_office_df.at[index,"production_companies"]=str(row['production_companies'][1:-1].split(',')[0].split(':')[1])

    if type(row['genres'])!=str or not row['genres']:
        lst.append(index)
    else:
        box_office_df.at[index,"genres"]=str(row['genres'][1:-1].split(',')[1].split(":")[1][:-1])

    if type(row['production_countries'])!=str or not row['production_countries']:
        lst.append(index)
    else:
        box_office_df.at[index,"production_countries"]=str(row['production_countries'][1:-1].split(',')[1].split(':')[1][:-1])

    # We can turn spoken languages into two columns: the spoken languages, and the number of spoken languages
    #  (can see if the number of spoken language increase its box office, and if so, what's the strongest language)

    # need to drop the columns whose budget is 0 

    # Replace original language with full name "English" instead of "en" (can do this with a dictionary of all the abbreviations)
    

    
box_office_df.drop(lst,inplace=True)

In[]:
# Basically just creating a datetime object and putting it into the columna and adding a column release_year with the year
for index, row in box_office_df.iterrows():
    date = row['release_date'].split('/')
    box_office_df.at[index,"release_date"]=datetime.datetime(2000+int(date[2]) if int(date[2])<=24 else 1900+int(date[2]),int(date[0]),int(date[1]))
    box_office_df.at[index,"release_year"]=2000+int(date[2]) if int(date[2])<=24 else 1900+int(date[2])

lst=[]

# Basically just creating a datetime object and putting it into the columna and adding a column release_year with the year
for index, row in rotten_tomatoes_movies_df.iterrows():
    if type(row['original_release_date'])!=str:
        lst.append(index)
    else:
        datetime_object = datetime.datetime.strptime(str(row['original_release_date']), '%Y-%m-%d')
        rotten_tomatoes_movies_df.at[index,"original_release_date"]=datetime_object
        rotten_tomatoes_movies_df.at[index,"release_year"]=datetime_object.year
rotten_tomatoes_movies_df.drop(lst)
rotten_tomatoes_movies_df
